### GET /oi

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/misc/get-open-interest

Retrieves the open interest for specified markets. This endpoint allows you to query the current open interest value for one or more markets identified by their unique hash.

## GET /oi

### Description
Retrieves the open interest for specified markets. This endpoint allows you to query the current open interest value for one or more markets identified by their unique hash.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/oi

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **market** (array of Hash64) - Required - A list of market hashes for which to retrieve open interest.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "market": ["0xdd22472e552920b8438158ea7238bfadfa4f736aa4cee91a6b86c39ead110917"]
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **market** (Hash64) - The unique hash of the market.
- **value** (number) - The current open interest value for the market.

#### Response Example
```json
[
  {
    "market": "0xdd22472e552920b8438158ea7238bfadfa4f736aa4cee91a6b86c39ead110917",
    "value": 1500.75
  }
]
```

#### Error Responses
- **400 Bad Request**: Indicates an issue with the request parameters.
- **500 Server Error**: Indicates a server-side problem.

### Get Active Orders with Market ID (Python)

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/CLOB/orders/get-active-order

Fetches active orders for a given market ID using the py_clob_client library. Requires a L2 header for authentication. The `market` parameter is used to filter the orders.

```python
from py_clob_client.clob_types import OpenOrderParams

resp = client.get_orders(
    OpenOrderParams(
        market="0xbd31dc8a20211944f6b70f31557f1001557b59905b7738480ca09bd4532f84af",
    )
)
print(resp)
print("Done!")
```

### GET /activity

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/core/get-user-activity

Retrieves on-chain activity for a specified user. Supports filtering by market, event, type, and time range, with options for sorting and pagination.

## GET /activity

### Description
Returns on-chain activity for a user. This endpoint allows for filtering by various parameters such as market, event, activity type, and time. It also supports sorting and pagination for efficient data retrieval.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/activity

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **limit** (integer) - Optional - Maximum number of results to return. Default: 100, Max: 500
- **offset** (integer) - Optional - Number of results to skip. Default: 0, Max: 10000
- **user** (Address) - Required - The user's profile address (0x-prefixed).
- **market** (array of Hash64) - Optional - Comma-separated list of condition IDs. Mutually exclusive with `eventId`.
- **eventId** (array of integer) - Optional - Comma-separated list of event IDs. Mutually exclusive with `market`.
- **type** (array of string) - Optional - Filters activity by type. Allowed values: TRADE, SPLIT, MERGE, REDEEM, REWARD, CONVERSION.
- **start** (integer) - Optional - Start timestamp for filtering activities.
- **end** (integer) - Optional - End timestamp for filtering activities.
- **sortBy** (string) - Optional - Field to sort the results by. Allowed values: TIMESTAMP, TOKENS, CASH. Default: TIMESTAMP.
- **sortDirection** (string) - Optional - Direction of sorting. Allowed values: ASC, DESC. Default: DESC.
- **side** (string) - Optional - Filters by trade side. Allowed values: BUY, SELL.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET /activity?user=0x56687bf447db6ffa42ffe2204a05edaa20f55839&limit=50&sortBy=TIMESTAMP&sortDirection=ASC"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **Array of Activity objects** - Each object contains details about a specific on-chain activity.

  - **proxyWallet** (Address) - The wallet address associated with the activity.
  - **timestamp** (integer) - The timestamp of the activity.
  - **conditionId** (Hash64) - The condition ID related to the activity.
  - **type** (string) - The type of activity (e.g., TRADE, REDEEM).
  - **size** (number) - The size of the activity.
  - **usdcSize** (number) - The size of the activity in USDC.
  - **transactionHash** (string) - The hash of the transaction.
  - **price** (number) - The price associated with the activity.
  - **asset** (string) - The asset involved in the activity.
  - **side** (string) - The side of the trade (BUY or SELL).
  - **outcomeIndex** (integer) - The index of the outcome.
  - **title** (string) - The title of the market.
  - **slug** (string) - The slug of the market.
  - **icon** (string) - The icon associated with the market.
  - **eventSlug** (string) - The slug of the event.
  - **outcome** (string) - The outcome of the event.
  - **name** (string) - The name of the event.
  - **pseudonym** (string) - The pseudonym of the user.
  - **bio** (string) - The bio of the user.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": [
    {
      "proxyWallet": "0x56687bf447db6ffa42ffe2204a05edaa20f55839",
      "timestamp": 1678886400,
      "conditionId": "0xdd22472e552920b8438158ea7238bfadfa4f736aa4cee91a6b86c39ead110917",
      "type": "TRADE",
      "size": 10,
      "usdcSize": 50,
      "transactionHash": "0xabc123...",
      "price": 0.5,
      "asset": "YES",
      "side": "BUY",
      "outcomeIndex": 0,
      "title": "Will ETH be above $2000 on March 15?",
      "slug": "eth-above-2000-march-15",
      "icon": "eth.png",
      "eventSlug": "eth-price-march-15",
      "outcome": "Yes",
      "name": "ETH Price Check",
      "pseudonym": "TraderJoe",
      "bio": "Crypto enthusiast"
    }
  ]
}
```

#### Error Responses
- **400 Bad Request**: Invalid query parameters or request format.
- **401 Unauthorized**: Authentication credentials are required and invalid.
- **500 Server Error**: An unexpected error occurred on the server.

### GET /trades

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/core/get-trades-for-a-user-or-markets

Retrieves a list of trades, optionally filtered by user or market.

## GET /trades

### Description
Retrieves a list of trades for a specific user or markets. Supports various filtering and pagination options.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/trades

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **limit** (integer) - Optional - Maximum number of trades to return (default: 100, max: 10000).
- **offset** (integer) - Optional - Number of trades to skip (default: 0, max: 10000).
- **takerOnly** (boolean) - Optional - Filter for trades where the user was the taker (default: true).
- **filterType** (string) - Optional - Filter trades by type ('CASH' or 'TOKENS'). Must be provided with `filterAmount`.
- **filterAmount** (number) - Optional - Filter trades by amount. Must be provided with `filterType`.
- **market** (array of Hash64) - Optional - Filter by a comma-separated list of market IDs. Mutually exclusive with `eventId`.
- **eventId** (array of integer) - Optional - Filter by a comma-separated list of event IDs. Mutually exclusive with `market`.
- **user** (Address) - Optional - Filter trades for a specific user address.
- **side** (string) - Optional - Filter trades by side ('BUY' or 'SELL').

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET /trades?limit=10&user=0x56687bf447db6ffa42ffe2204a05edaa20f55839&side=BUY"
}
```

#### Success Response (200)
- **Array of Trade objects**
  - **proxyWallet** (Address) - The wallet address of the proxy.
  - **side** (string) - The side of the trade ('BUY' or 'SELL').
  - **asset** (string) - The asset traded.
  - **conditionId** (Hash64) - The condition ID of the trade.
  - **size** (number) - The size of the trade.
  - **price** (number) - The price of the trade.
  - **timestamp** (integer) - The timestamp of the trade.
  - **title** (string) - The title of the event.
  - **slug** (string) - The slug of the event.
  - **icon** (string) - The icon for the event.
  - **eventSlug** (string) - The slug of the event.
  - **outcome** (string) - The outcome of the event.
  - **outcomeIndex** (integer) - The index of the outcome.
  - **name** (string) - The name of the market.
  - **pseudonym** (string) - Pseudonym of the user.
  - **bio** (string) - Bio of the user.
  - **profileImage** (string) - Profile image URL.
  - **profileImageOptimized** (string) - Optimized profile image URL.
  - **transactionHash** (string) - The transaction hash associated with the trade.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": [
    {
      "proxyWallet": "0x56687bf447db6ffa42ffe2204a05edaa20f55839",
      "side": "BUY",
```

### Configure CLOB Client with Remote Signing Server

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/builders/builder-signing-server

Integrates the CLOB Client with the Builder Signing Server for secure order attribution. This setup ensures that API keys remain on the signing server, enhancing security.

```typescript
import { ClobClient } from "@polymarket/clob-client";
import { BuilderConfig } from "@polymarket/builder-signing-sdk";

const builderConfig = new BuilderConfig({
    remoteBuilderConfig: {url: "http://localhost:3000/sign"}
});

const clobClient = new ClobClient(
    host,
    chainId,
    wallet,
    creds,
    SignatureType.POLY_PROXY,
    funderAddress,
    undefined,
    false,
    builderConfig
);

// Orders will automatically use the signing server
const order = await clobClient.createOrder({
    price: 0.40,
    side: Side.BUY,
    size: 5,
    tokenID: "27072675915285915455116137912884489109876947142577610372904917850067886308458"
});

const response = await clobClient.postOrder(order);
```

--------------------------------

### Get Midpoint Price OpenAPI Specification

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/pricing/get-midpoint-price

This OpenAPI specification defines the GET /midpoint endpoint for the CLOB API. It allows users to retrieve the midpoint price for a specific token by providing its unique token_id. The response includes the midpoint price or detailed error information for invalid requests, missing orderbooks, or server errors.

```yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: CLOB (Central Limit Order Book) API
  description: >-
    API for interacting with the Central Limit Order Book system, providing
    orderbook data, prices, midpoints, and spreads
  version: 1.0.0
  contact:
    name: CLOB API Team
  license:
    name: MIT
servers:
  - url: https://clob.polymarket.com/
    description: Production server
security: []
tags:
  - name: Orderbook
    description: Order book related operations
  - name: Pricing
    description: Price and midpoint operations
  - name: Spreads
    description: Spread calculation operations
paths:
  /midpoint:
    get:
      tags:
        - Pricing
      summary: Get midpoint price
      description: Retrieves the midpoint price for a specific token
      parameters:
        - name: token_id
          in: query
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
          description: The unique identifier for the token
          example: '1234567890'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Successful response
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/MidpointResponse'
        '400':
          description: Bad request
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'
              example:
                error: Invalid token id
        '404':
          description: Order book not found
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'
              example:
                error: No orderbook exists for the requested token id
        '500':
          description: Internal server error
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Error'
components:
  schemas:
    MidpointResponse:
      type: object
      required:
        - mid
      properties:
        mid:
          type: string
          description: The midpoint price (as string to maintain precision)
          example: '1800.75'
    Error:
      type: object
      required:
        - error
      properties:
        error:
          type: string
          description: Error message describing what went wrong
          example: Invalid token id

```

--------------------------------

### Get Market Price

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/pricing/get-market-price

Retrieves the market price for a specific token and side. This endpoint is part of the CLOB API, which handles order book operations and pricing.

## GET /price

### Description
Retrieves the market price for a specific token and side.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/price

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **token_id** (string) - Required - The unique identifier for the token.
- **side** (string) - Required - The side of the market (BUY or SELL).

### Request Example
```json
{
  "token_id": "1234567890",
  "side": "BUY"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **price** (string) - The market price (as string to maintain precision).

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "price": "1800.50"
}
```

#### Error Responses
- **400 Bad Request**: Returned for invalid token ID or side.
  - Example:
    ```json
    {
      "error": "Invalid token id"
    }
    ```
- **404 Not Found**: Returned if no order book exists for the requested token ID.
  - Example:
    ```json
    {
      "error": "No orderbook exists for the requested token id"
    }
    ```
- **500 Internal Server Error**: Returned for unexpected server errors.

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/CLOB/quickstart

This code snippet illustrates how to resolve the `L2_AUTH_NOT_AVAILABLE` error by ensuring that API credentials are created or derived before initializing the CLOB client. This is crucial for proper authentication in L2 environments.

```typescript
const creds = await clobClient.createOrDeriveApiKey();
const client = new ClobClient(host, chainId, wallet, creds);

```

### Get Total Markets Traded by User

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/misc/get-total-markets-a-user-has-traded

Retrieves the total number of markets a specific user has traded on Polymarket. Requires the user's address as a query parameter.

## GET /traded

### Description
Retrieves the total number of markets a specific user has traded on Polymarket. Requires the user's address as a query parameter.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/traded

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **user** (string) - Required - User Profile Address (0x-prefixed, 40 hex chars)

### Request Example
```json
{
  "user": "0x56687bf447db6ffa42ffe2204a05edaa20f55839"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **user** (string) - User Profile Address.
- **traded** (integer) - Total number of markets traded by the user.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "user": "0x56687bf447db6ffa42ffe2204a05edaa20f55839",
  "traded": 150
}
```

#### Error Response (400, 401, 500)
- **error** (string) - Description of the error.

#### Error Response Example
```json
{
  "error": "Invalid user address format"
}
```

### POST /books - Get multiple order book summaries

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/orderbook/get-multiple-order-books-summaries-by-request

Retrieves order book summaries for specified tokens via a POST request. This endpoint allows fetching summaries for up to 500 tokens in a single request.

## POST /books

### Description
Retrieves order book summaries for specified tokens via POST request. Allows fetching summaries for up to 500 tokens in a single request.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/books

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **Array of BookRequest objects** (array) - Required - An array of objects, where each object contains a `token_id` and an optional `side`. The array can contain a maximum of 500 items.
  - **token_id** (string) - Required - The unique identifier for the token.
  - **side** (string) - Optional - Enum: BUY, SELL. Optional side parameter for certain operations.

### Request Example
```json
[
  {
    "token_id": "1234567890",
    "side": "BUY"
  },
  {
    "token_id": "0987654321"
  }
]
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **Array of OrderBookSummary objects** (array) - An array containing order book summaries for the requested tokens.
  - **market** (string) - Market identifier.
  - **asset_id** (string) - Asset identifier.
  - **timestamp** (string) - Timestamp of the order book snapshot (date-time format).
  - **hash** (string) - Hash of the order book state.
  - **bids** (array) - Array of bid levels, each with `price` (string) and `size` (string).
  - **asks** (array) - Array of ask levels, each with `price` (string) and `size` (string).
  - **min_order_size** (string) - Minimum order size for this market.
  - **tick_size** (string) - Minimum price increment.
  - **neg_risk** (boolean) - Whether negative risk is enabled.

#### Response Example (Success)
```json
[
  {
    "market": "0x1b6f76e5b8587ee896c35847e12d11e75290a8c3934c5952e8a9d6e4c6f03cfa",
    "asset_id": "1234567890",
    "timestamp": "2023-10-01T12:00:00Z",
    "hash": "0xabc123def456...",
    "bids": [
      {
        "price": "1800.50",
        "size": "10.5"
      }
    ],
    "asks": [
      {
        "price": "1801.00",
        "size": "5.2"
      }
    ],
    "min_order_size": "0.001",
    "tick_size": "0.01",
    "neg_risk": false
  }
]
```

#### Error Response (400)
- **Error object** (object) - Returned when the payload is invalid or exceeds the limit.
  - **error** (string) - Error message describing what went wrong.

#### Response Example (Error - Invalid Payload)
```json
{
  "error": "Invalid payload"
}
```

#### Response Example (Error - Exceeds Limit)
```json
{
  "error": "Payload exceeds the limit"
}
```

#### Error Response (500)
- **Error object** (object) - Returned for internal server errors.
  - **error** (string) - Error message describing what went wrong.

#### Response Example (Error - Internal Server Error)
```json
{
  "error": "Internal server error"
}
```

### Initialize ClobClient for Creating and Posting Orders (TypeScript, Python)

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/CLOB/clients/methods-overview

Initializes the ClobClient for creating and posting orders. This requires a signer, API credentials, signature type, and optionally a funder address for Gnosis Safe proxies. It provides access to all public, L1, and L2 methods for order management and trade retrieval.

```TypeScript
const client = new ClobClient(
  "https://clob.polymarket.com", 
  137, 
  signer,
  creds,
  2, // Indicates Gnosis Safe proxy
  funder // Safe wallet address holding funds
);

// All public, L1, and L2 methods available
const order = await client.createOrder({ /* ... */ });
const result = await client.postOrder(order);
const trades = await client.getTrades();
```

```Python
const client = new ClobClient(
    host="https://clob.polymarket.com",
    chain_id=137,
    key="private_key",
    creds=creds,
    signature_type=2, // Indicates Gnosis Safe proxy
    funder="funder_address" // Safe wallet address holding funds
)

# All public, L1, and L2 methods available
order = client.create_order({ /* ... */ })
result = client.post_order(order)
trades = client.get_trades()
```

### Set Token Approvals

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/builders/relayer-client

Sets token allowances for specific protocols, enabling trading. This example shows approving USDC spending for the Conditional Token Framework (CTF).

## Set Token Approvals

### Description
Sets token allowances to enable trading. This example approves USDC spending for the Conditional Token Framework.

### Method
POST (implied by client.execute() which is an asynchronous operation)

### Endpoint
/websites/polymarket/approve (inferred)

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **tokenAddress** (string) - The address of the token to approve.
- **spenderAddress** (string) - The address of the spender.
- **amount** (string) - The amount to approve (e.g., `ethers.constants.MaxUint256`).

### Request Example
```typescript
import { ethers } from "ethers";
import { Interface } from "ethers/lib/utils";
import { Transaction } from "@polymarket/builder-relayer-client";

const erc20Interface = new Interface([
    {
      "constant": false,
      "inputs": [
          {"name": "_spender", "type": "address"},
          {"name": "_value", "type": "uint256"}
      ],
      "name": "approve",
      "outputs": [{"name": "", "type": "bool"}],
      "payable": false,
      "stateMutability": "nonpayable",
      "type": "function"
  }
]);

function createApprovalTransaction(
    tokenAddress: string,
    spenderAddress: string
): Transaction {
    return {
        to: tokenAddress,
        data: erc20Interface.encodeFunctionData("approve", [
            spenderAddress,
            ethers.constants.MaxUint256
        ]),
        value: "0"
    };
}

const usdcAddress = "0x2791Bca1f2de4661ED88A30C99A7a9449Aa84174";
const ctfAddress = "0x4d97dcd97ec945f40cf65f87097ace5ea0476045";

const approvalTx = createApprovalTransaction(usdcAddress, ctfAddress);
const response = await client.execute(
    [approvalTx],
    "Approve USDC for CTF"
);

const result = await response.wait();
console.log("Approval completed:", result?.transactionHash);
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **transactionHash** (string) - The hash of the approval transaction.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "transactionHash": "0xabc123..."
}
```

### Book Message

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/CLOB/websocket/market-channel

Details about the 'book' message, including its structure, when it's emitted, and an example response.

## Book Message

### Description
Emitted when first subscribed to a market or when there is a trade that affects the order book.

### Event Type
`book`

### Structure
* **event_type** (string): Must be "book".
* **asset_id** (string): The unique identifier for the asset.
* **market** (string): The condition ID of the market.
* **timestamp** (string): Unix timestamp in milliseconds indicating when the book was generated.
* **hash** (string): A hash summarizing the order book content.
* **buys** (OrderSummary[]): A list of aggregate buy orders at different price levels.
* **sells** (OrderSummary[]): A list of aggregate sell orders at different price levels.

`OrderSummary` Object:
* **price** (string): The price level of the order.
* **size** (string): The aggregate size available at that price level.

### Response Example (Success - 200)
```json
{
  "event_type": "book",
  "asset_id": "65818619657568813474341868652308942079804919287380422192892211131408793125422",
  "market": "0xbd31dc8a20211944f6b70f31557f1001557b59905b7738480ca09bd4532f84af",
  "bids": [
    { "price": ".48", "size": "30" },
    { "price": ".49", "size": "20" },
    { "price": ".50", "size": "15" }
  ],
  "asks": [
    { "price": ".52", "size": "25" },
    { "price": ".53", "size": "60" },
    { "price": ".54", "size": "10" }
  ],
  "timestamp": "123456789000",
  "hash": "0x0...."
}
```

### Fetch All Active Markets via Events Endpoint

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/gamma-markets-api/fetch-markets-guide

Efficiently retrieve all active markets by querying the events endpoint and working backwards. This approach is suitable for broader market discovery.

## GET /events

### Description
Fetches a list of events, useful for retrieving all active markets. Supports ordering, filtering by closed status, and pagination.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/events`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **order** (string) - Optional - Specifies the order of results. Use `id` to order by event ID.
- **ascending** (boolean) - Optional - Determines the sort direction. `false` for newest first.
- **closed** (boolean) - Optional - Filters for active markets (`false`) or closed markets (`true`).
- **limit** (integer) - Optional - The number of results to return per page.
- **offset** (integer) - Optional - The number of results to skip for pagination.

### Request Example
```bash
curl "https://gamma-api.polymarket.com/events?order=id&ascending=false&closed=false&limit=100"
```

### Pagination
Use `limit` and `offset` parameters to paginate through large datasets.

#### Pagination Examples
```bash
# Page 1: First 50 results (offset=0)
curl "https://gamma-api.polymarket.com/events?order=id&ascending=false&closed=false&limit=50&offset=0"

# Page 2: Next 50 results (offset=50)
curl "https://gamma-api.polymarket.com/events?order=id&ascending=false&closed=false&limit=50&offset=50"

# Page 3: Next 50 results (offset=100)
curl "https://gamma-api.polymarket.com/events?order=id&ascending=false&closed=false&limit=50&offset=100"
```

### Set Token Approvals

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/builders/relayer-client

Sets token allowances to enable trading. This example approves USDC spending for the Conditional Token Framework. It requires the ERC20 interface and defines a function to create the approval transaction.

```typescript
import { ethers } from "ethers";
import { Interface } from "ethers/lib/utils";
import { Transaction } from "@polymarket/builder-relayer-client";

// Define ERC20 approval interface
const erc20Interface = new Interface([
    {
        "constant": false,
        "inputs": [
            {"name": "_spender", "type": "address"},
            {"name": "_value", "type": "uint256"}
        ],
        "name": "approve",
        "outputs": [{"name": "", "type": "bool"}],
        "payable": false,
        "stateMutability": "nonpayable",
        "type": "function"
    }
]);

// Create approval transaction
function createApprovalTransaction(
    tokenAddress: string,
    spenderAddress: string
): Transaction {
    return {
        to: tokenAddress,
        data: erc20Interface.encodeFunctionData("approve", [
            spenderAddress,
            ethers.constants.MaxUint256
        ]),
        value: "0"
    };
}

// Execute the approval
const usdcAddress = "0x2791Bca1f2de4661ED88A30C99A7a9449Aa84174";
const ctfAddress = "0x4d97dcd97ec945f40cf65f87097ace5ea0476045";

const approvalTx = createApprovalTransaction(usdcAddress, ctfAddress);
const response = await client.execute(
    [approvalTx],
    "Approve USDC for CTF"
);

const result = await response.wait();
console.log("Approval completed:", result?.transactionHash);
```

### Get Traded Markets (OpenAPI)

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/misc/get-total-markets-a-user-has-traded

This OpenAPI specification defines the 'get /traded' endpoint for the Polymarket Data API. It allows clients to retrieve the total number of markets a user has traded by providing the user's address as a query parameter. The response includes the user's address and the count of markets traded. Error responses are also defined for various scenarios like bad requests or unauthorized access.

```yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: Polymarket Data API
  version: 1.0.0
  description: >
    HTTP API for Polymarket data. This specification documents all public
    routes.
servers:
  - url: https://data-api.polymarket.com
    description: Relative server (same host)
security: []
tags:
  - name: Health
  - name: Core
  - name: Builders
  - name: Misc
paths:
  /traded:
    get:
      tags:
        - Misc
      summary: Get total markets a user has traded
      parameters:
        - in: query
          name: user
          required: true
          schema:
            $ref: '#/components/schemas/Address'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Success
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Traded'
        '400':
          description: Bad Request
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/ErrorResponse'
        '401':
          description: Unauthorized
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/ErrorResponse'
        '500':
          description: Server Error
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/ErrorResponse'
components:
  schemas:
    Address:
      type: string
      description: User Profile Address (0x-prefixed, 40 hex chars)
      pattern: '^0x[a-fA-F0-9]{40}$'
      example: '0x56687bf447db6ffa42ffe2204a05edaa20f55839'
    Traded:
      type: object
      properties:
        user:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/Address'
        traded:
          type: integer
    ErrorResponse:
      type: object
      properties:
        error:
          type: string
      required:
        - error

```

```bash
# POLY_BUILDER_SECRET
```

### Get Event by ID - OpenAPI Specification (YAML)

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/events/get-event-by-id

This OpenAPI definition specifies the 'get /events/{id}' endpoint for retrieving event details. It includes parameters for filtering and optional data inclusions, and defines the structure of the 'Event' response object. It relies on a shared 'pathId' parameter definition.

```yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: Markets API
  version: 1.0.0
  description: REST API specification for public endpoints used by the Markets service.
servers:
  - url: https://gamma-api.polymarket.com
    description: Polymarket Gamma API Production Server
security: []
tags:
  - name: Health
    description: Health check endpoints
  - name: Sports
    description: Sports-related endpoints including teams and game data
  - name: Tags
    description: Tag management and related tag operations
  - name: Events
    description: Event management and event-related operations
  - name: Markets
    description: Market data and market-related operations
  - name: Comments
    description: Comment system and user interactions
  - name: Series
    description: Series management and related operations
  - name: Profiles
    description: User profile management
  - name: Search
    description: Search functionality across different entity types
paths:
  /events/{id}:
    get:
      tags:
        - Events
      summary: Get event by id
      operationId: getEvent
      parameters:
        - $ref: '#/components/parameters/pathId'
        - name: include_chat
          in: query
          schema:
            type: boolean
        - name: include_template
          in: query
          schema:
            type: boolean
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Event
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/Event'
        '404':
          description: Not found
components:
  parameters:
    pathId:
      name: id
      in: path
      required: true
      schema:
        type: integer
  schemas:
    Event:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
        ticker:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        slug:

          type: string

          type: boolean
          nullable: true

          type: boolean

          type: boolean

          nullable: true

          type: number
          nullable: true

          type: number
```

### GET /getTickSize

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/CLOB/clients/methods-public

Retrieves the tick size (minimum price increment) for a market.

## GET /getTickSize

### Description
Get the tick size (minimum price increment) for a market.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/getTickSize

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **tokenID** (string) - Required - The ID of the token.

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **TickSize** (string) - The tick size, which can be '0.1', '0.01', '0.001', or '0.0001'.

#### Response Example
```json
"0.01"
```

--------------------------------

### GET /getLastTradesPrices

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/CLOB/clients/methods-public

Retrieves the prices of the most recent trades for multiple tokens.

## GET /getLastTradesPrices

### Description
Get the price of the most recent trade for a token.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/getLastTradesPrices

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **params** (BookParams[]) - Required - An array of objects, where each object contains `token_id` and `side`.
  - **token_id** (string) - Required - The ID of the token.
  - **side** (Side) - Required - The side of the trade (e.g., 'buy' or 'sell').

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **LastTradePriceWithToken[]** - An array of objects, each containing `price`, `side`, and `token_id` for the last trade of each token.

#### Response Example
```json
[
  { "price": "1.50", "side": "buy", "token_id": "0x123..." },
  { "price": "2.10", "side": "sell", "token_id": "0x456..." }
]
```

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/builders/builder-signing-server

Demonstrates how to configure a client application to use the Builder Signing Server by specifying its URL. This ensures that requests are directed to the correct signing endpoint.

```typescript
// In your client application
const builderConfig = new BuilderConfig({
    remoteBuilderConfig: {url: "http://localhost:3000/sign"}
});
```

```typescript
interface OpenOrder {
  id: string;
```

### Fetch Markets/Events by Tags

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/gamma-markets-api/fetch-markets-guide

Filter markets and events by category or topic using tag IDs. You can discover available tags through dedicated endpoints.

## GET /tags

### Description
Retrieves a list of general available tags.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/tags`

## GET /sports

### Description
Retrieves comprehensive metadata for sports, including tag IDs.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/sports`

## GET /markets

### Description
Fetches a list of markets, with options to filter by tag.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/markets`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **tag_id** (string) - Optional - Filters markets by a specific tag ID.
- **related_tags** (boolean) - Optional - Includes markets related to the specified tag.
- **exclude_tag_id** (string) - Optional - Excludes markets with a specific tag ID.
- **closed** (boolean) - Optional - Filters for active (false) or closed (true) markets.
- **limit** (integer) - Optional - Number of results to return per page.
- **offset** (integer) - Optional - Number of results to skip for pagination.

### Request Example
```bash
curl "https://gamma-api.polymarket.com/markets?tag_id=100381&closed=false&limit=1&offset=0"
```

## GET /events

### Description
Fetches a list of events, with options to filter by tag.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/events`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **tag_id** (string) - Optional - Filters events by a specific tag ID.
- **related_tags** (boolean) - Optional - Includes events related to the specified tag.
- **exclude_tag_id** (string) - Optional - Excludes events with a specific tag ID.
- **closed** (boolean) - Optional - Filters for active (false) or closed (true) events.
- **limit** (integer) - Optional - Number of results to return per page.
- **offset** (integer) - Optional - Number of results to skip for pagination.

### Request Example
```bash
curl "https://gamma-api.polymarket.com/events?tag_id=100381&limit=1&closed=false"
```

### GET /series/{id}

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/series/get-series-by-id

Retrieves a specific series by its ID. Supports optional query parameters to include chat information.

## GET /series/{id}

### Description
Retrieves a specific series by its ID. Supports optional query parameters to include chat information.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/series/{id}

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **id** (integer) - Required - The unique identifier for the series.

#### Query Parameters
- **include_chat** (boolean) - Optional - If true, includes chat information in the response.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET /series/123?include_chat=true"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The unique identifier for the series.
- **ticker** (string) - The ticker symbol for the series.
- **slug** (string) - The slug for the series.
- **title** (string) - The title of the series.
- **subtitle** (string) - The subtitle of the series.
- **seriesType** (string) - The type of the series.
- **recurrence** (string) - The recurrence pattern of the series.
- **description** (string) - A description of the series.
- **image** (string) - URL to the series image.
- **icon** (string) - URL to the series icon.
- **layout** (string) - The layout type for the series.
- **active** (boolean) - Indicates if the series is active.
- **closed** (boolean) - Indicates if the series is closed.
- **archived** (boolean) - Indicates if the series is archived.
- **new** (boolean) - Indicates if the series is new.
- **featured** (boolean) - Indicates if the series is featured.
- **restricted** (boolean) - Indicates if the series is restricted.
- **isTemplate** (boolean) - Indicates if the series is a template.
- **templateVariables** (boolean) - Indicates if the series has template variables.
- **publishedAt** (string) - The publication date of the series.
- **createdBy** (string) - The user who created the series.
- **updatedBy** (string) - The user who last updated the series.
- **createdAt** (string) - The creation timestamp of the series.
- **updatedAt** (string) - The last update timestamp of the series.
- **commentsEnabled** (boolean) - Indicates if comments are enabled for the series.
- **competitive** (string) - Competitive nature of the series.
- **volume24hr** (number) - Trading volume in the last 24 hours.
- **volume** (number) - Total trading volume.
- **liquidity** (number) - Liquidity of the series.
- **startDate** (string) - The start date of the series.
- **pythTokenID** (string) - The Pyth token ID associated with the series.
- **cgAssetName** (string) - The CoinGecko asset name.
- **score** (integer) - The score of the series.
- **events** (array) - An array of events related to the series.
- **collections** (array) - An array of collections the series belongs to.
- **categories** (array) - An array of categories the series belongs to.
- **tags** (array) - An array of tags associated with the series.
- **commentCount** (integer) - The number of comments on the series.
- **chats** (array) - An array of chats related to the series.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": "{\n  \"id\": \"42\",\n  \"ticker\": \"XYZ\",\n  \"slug\": \"example-series\",\n  \"title\": \"Example Series Title\",\n  \"subtitle\": \"A detailed subtitle for the example series\",\n  \"seriesType\": \"REGULAR\",\n  \"recurrence\": \"DAILY\",\n  \"description\": \"This is a comprehensive description of the example series.\",\n  \"image\": \"https://example.com/image.png\",\n  \"icon\": \"https://example.com/icon.png\",\n  \"layout\": \"GRID\",\n  \"active\": true,\n  \"closed\": false,\n  \"archived\": false,\n  \"new\": false,\n  \"featured\": true,\n  \"restricted\": false,\n  \"isTemplate\": false,\n  \"templateVariables\": false,\n  \"publishedAt\": \"2023-10-27T10:00:00Z\",\n  \"createdBy\": \"user123\",\n  \"updatedBy\": \"user456\",\n  \"createdAt\": \"2023-10-26T09:00:00Z\",\n  \"updatedAt\": \"2023-10-27T09:30:00Z\",\n  \"commentsEnabled\": true,\n  \"competitive\": \"HIGH\",\n  \"volume24hr\": 100000.50,\n  \"volume\": 500000.75,\n  \"liquidity\": 2000.00,\n  \"startDate\": \"2023-10-28T12:00:00Z\",\n  \"pythTokenID\": \"pyth_abc123\",\n  \"cgAssetName\": \"example-coin\",\n  \"score\": 85,\n  \"events\": [],\n  \"collections\": [],\n  \"categories\": [],\n  \"tags\": [],\n  \"commentCount\": 50,\n  \"chats\": []\n}"}
```

### Initialize Polymarket Relayer Client (TypeScript)

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/builders/relayer-client

Initializes the Polymarket Relayer Client using Ethers v5 or Viem. Requires environment variables for relayer URL, chain ID, private key, and builder API credentials. Supports standard, safe, and proxy wallet transaction types.

```typescript
import { ethers } from "ethers";
import { RelayClient, RelayerTxType } from "@polymarket/builder-relayer-client";
import { BuilderApiKeyCreds, BuilderConfig } from "@polymarket/builder-signing-sdk";

const relayerUrl = process.env.POLYMARKET_RELAYER_URL;
const chainId = 137; // Polygon mainnet

// Create wallet
const provider = new ethers.providers.JsonRpcProvider(process.env.RPC_URL);
const wallet = new ethers.Wallet(process.env.PRIVATE_KEY, provider);

// Configure builder credentials
const builderCreds: BuilderApiKeyCreds = {
    key: process.env.BUILDER_API_KEY!,
    secret: process.env.BUILDER_SECRET!,
    passphrase: process.env.BUILDER_PASS_PHRASE!
};

const builderConfig = new BuilderConfig({
    localBuilderCreds: builderCreds
});

// Initialize client
const client = new RelayClient(relayerUrl, chainId, wallet, builderConfig);
// or explicitly:
const safeClient = new RelayClient(relayerUrl, chainId, wallet, builderConfig, RelayerTxType.SAFE);

// For Proxy Wallets (Magic Link users)
const proxyClient = new RelayClient(relayerUrl, chainId, wallet, builderConfig, RelayerTxType.PROXY);
```

```typescript
import { createWalletClient, http, Hex } from "viem";
import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
import { polygon } from "viem/chains";
import { RelayClient, RelayerTxType } from "@polymarket/builder-relayer-client";
import { BuilderApiKeyCreds, BuilderConfig } from "@polymarket/builder-signing-sdk";

const relayerUrl = process.env.POLYMARKET_RELAYER_URL;
const chainId = 137; // Polygon mainnet

// Create wallet
const account = privateKeyToAccount(process.env.PRIVATE_KEY as Hex);
const wallet = createWalletClient({
    account,
    chain: polygon,
    transport: http(process.env.RPC_URL)
});

// Configure builder credentials
const builderCreds: BuilderApiKeyCreds = {
    key: process.env.BUILDER_API_KEY!,
    secret: process.env.BUILDER_SECRET!,
    passphrase: process.env.BUILDER_PASS_PHRASE!
};

const builderConfig = new BuilderConfig({
    localBuilderCreds: builderCreds
});

// Initialize client
const client = new RelayClient(relayerUrl, chainId, wallet, builderConfig);
// or explicitly:
const safeClient = new RelayClient(relayerUrl, chainId, wallet, builderConfig, RelayerTxType.SAFE);

// For Proxy Wallets (Magic Link users)
const proxyClient = new RelayClient(relayerUrl, chainId, wallet, builderConfig, RelayerTxType.PROXY);
```

### GET /markets/slug/{slug}

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/markets/get-market-by-slug

Retrieves a specific market's data using its unique slug. This endpoint is part of the Markets API.

## GET /markets/slug/{slug}

### Description
Retrieves a specific market by its slug. This endpoint allows you to fetch detailed information about a market, including its question, outcomes, and liquidity.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/markets/slug/{slug}`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **slug** (string) - Required - The unique identifier (slug) of the market.

#### Query Parameters
- **include_tag** (boolean) - Optional - Whether to include tag information in the response.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET /markets/slug/example-market-slug?include_tag=true"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The unique identifier of the market.
- **question** (string) - The question posed by the market.
- **conditionId** (string) - The ID of the market's condition.
- **slug** (string) - The slug of the market.
- **twitterCardImage** (string) - URL for the Twitter card image.
- **resolutionSource** (string) - The source for market resolution.
- **endDate** (string) - The end date of the market (ISO 8601 format).
- **category** (string) - The category the market belongs to.
- **ammType** (string) - The Automated Market Maker type.
- **liquidity** (string) - The amount of liquidity in the market.
- **sponsorName** (string) - The name of the market sponsor.
- **sponsorImage** (string) - URL for the sponsor's image.
- **startDate** (string) - The start date of the market (ISO 8601 format).
- **xAxisValue** (string) - Value for the x-axis.
- **yAxisValue** (string) - Value for the y-axis.
- **denominationToken** (string) - The denomination token used.
- **fee** (string) - The fee associated with the market.
- **image** (string) - URL for the market image.
- **icon** (string) - URL for the market icon.
- **lowerBound** (string) - The lower bound of the market range.
- **upperBound** (string) - The upper bound of the market range.
- **description** (string) - A description of the market.
- **outcomes** (string) - Information about the market outcomes.
- **outcomePrices** (string) - Prices of the market outcomes.
- **volume** (string) - The trading volume of the market.
- **active** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is active.
- **marketType** (string) - The type of market.
- **formatType** (string) - The format type of the market.
- **lowerBoundDate** (string) - The date for the lower bound.
- **upperBoundDate** (string) - The date for the upper bound.
- **closed** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is closed.
- **marketMakerAddress** (string) - The address of the market maker.
- **createdBy** (integer) - The ID of the user who created the market.
- **updatedBy** (integer) - The ID of the user who last updated the market.
- **createdAt** (string) - The creation timestamp (ISO 8601 format).
- **updatedAt** (string) - The last update timestamp (ISO 8601 format).
- **closedTime** (string) - The timestamp when the market was closed.
- **wideFormat** (boolean) - Indicates if the market uses a wide format.
- **new** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is new.
- **mailchimpTag** (string) - Mailchimp tag associated with the market.
- **featured** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is featured.
- **archived** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is archived.
- **resolvedBy** (string) - The entity that resolved the market.
- **restricted** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is restricted.
- **marketGroup** (integer) - The market group ID.
- **groupItemTitle** (string) - The title for the market group item.
- **groupItemThreshold** (string) - The threshold for the market group item.
- **questionID** (string) - The ID of the question associated with the market.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "mk_a1b2c3d4e5f6",
  "question": "Will Bitcoin reach $70,000 by December 31, 2024?",
  "conditionId": "cond_xyz789",

  "groupItemTitle": "",
  "groupItemThreshold": "",
  "questionID": "q_abc123"
}
```

#### Error Response (404)
- **description**: Not found

### Get Event by Slug

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/events/get-event-by-slug

## GET /events/slug/{slug}

### Description
Retrieves details for a specific event using its unique slug. Supports optional query parameters to include chat and template information.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/events/slug/{slug}

#### Path Parameters
- **slug** (string) - Required - The unique identifier for the event.

#### Query Parameters
- **include_chat** (boolean) - Optional - Whether to include chat information in the response.
- **include_template** (boolean) - Optional - Whether to include template information in the response.

### Request Example

```json
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The unique identifier of the event.
- **ticker** (string) - The ticker symbol for the event (nullable).
- **slug** (string) - The slug of the event (nullable).
- **title** (string) - The title of the event (nullable).
- **subtitle** (string) - The subtitle of the event (nullable).
- **description** (string) - The description of the event (nullable).
- **resolutionSource** (string) - The source for event resolution (nullable).
- **startDate** (string) - The start date and time of the event (nullable).
- **creationDate** (string) - The creation date and time of the event (nullable).
- **endDate** (string) - The end date and time of the event (nullable).
- **image** (string) - URL of the event image (nullable).
- **icon** (string) - URL of the event icon (nullable).
- **active** (boolean) - Indicates if the event is active (nullable).
- **closed** (boolean) - Indicates if the event is closed (nullable).
- **archived** (boolean) - Indicates if the event is archived (nullable).
- **new** (boolean) - Indicates if the event is new (nullable).
- **featured** (boolean) - Indicates if the event is featured (nullable).
- **restricted** (boolean) - Indicates if the event is restricted (nullable).
- **liquidity** (number) - The liquidity of the event (nullable).
- **volume** (number) - The trading volume of the event (nullable).
- **openInterest** (number) - The open interest for the event (nullable).
- **sortBy** (string) - Sorting criteria for the event (nullable).
- **category** (string) - The category of the event (nullable).
- **subcategory** (string) - The subcategory of the event (nullable).
- **isTemplate** (boolean) - Indicates if the event is a template (nullable).
- **templateVariables** (string) - Template variables for the event (nullable).

- **createdBy** (string) - The identifier of the user who created the event (nullable).

### GET /websites/polymarket

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/events/get-event-by-id

Retrieves a list of markets with detailed information including trading volumes, liquidity, fees, and status.

## GET /websites/polymarket

### Description
Retrieves a list of markets with detailed information including trading volumes, liquidity, fees, and status. This endpoint provides access to various metrics like 24-hour volume, liquidity, maker/taker fees, and order acceptance status.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/websites/polymarket

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **id** (string) - Optional - The unique identifier for a market.
- **slug** (string) - Optional - The URL-friendly identifier for a market.

### Request Example
GET /websites/polymarket?slug=example-market

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The unique identifier of the market.
- **title** (string) - The title of the market.
- **volume24hrClob** (number) - The 24-hour trading volume on the CLOB exchange.
- **volume1wkClob** (number) - The 1-week trading volume on the CLOB exchange.
- **volume1moClob** (number) - The 1-month trading volume on the CLOB exchange.
- **volume1yrClob** (number) - The 1-year trading volume on the CLOB exchange.
- **volumeAmm** (number) - The trading volume on the AMM exchange.
- **volumeClob** (number) - The total trading volume on the CLOB exchange.
- **liquidityAmm** (number) - The liquidity provided by the AMM exchange.
- **liquidityClob** (number) - The liquidity provided by the CLOB exchange.
- **makerBaseFee** (integer) - The base fee for makers.
- **takerBaseFee** (integer) - The base fee for takers.
- **customLiveness** (integer) - Custom liveness parameter for the market.
- **acceptingOrders** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is currently accepting orders.
- **notificationsEnabled** (boolean) - Indicates if notifications are enabled for the market.
- **score** (integer) - A score representing the market's performance or relevance.
- **imageOptimized** (object) - Optimized image details for the market.
- **iconOptimized** (object) - Optimized icon details for the market.
- **events** (array) - A list of events associated with the market.
- **categories** (array) - A list of categories the market belongs to.
- **tags** (array) - A list of tags associated with the market.
- **creator** (string) - The creator of the market.
- **ready** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is ready.
- **funded** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is funded.
- **pastSlugs** (string) - Historical slugs for the market.
- **readyTimestamp** (string) - Timestamp when the market became ready.
- **fundedTimestamp** (string) - Timestamp when the market was funded.
- **acceptingOrdersTimestamp** (string) - Timestamp when the market started accepting orders.
- **competitive** (number) - A measure of market competitiveness.
- **rewardsMinSize** (number) - The minimum size for rewards.
- **rewardsMaxSpread** (number) - The maximum spread for rewards.
- **spread** (number) - The current spread of the market.
- **automaticallyResolved** (boolean) - Indicates if the market resolves automatically.
- **oneDayPriceChange** (number) - The price change in the last 24 hours.
- **oneHourPriceChange** (number) - The price change in the last hour.
- **oneWeekPriceChange** (number) - The price change in the last week.
- **oneMonthPriceChange** (number) - The price change in the last month.
- **oneYearPriceChange** (number) - The price change in the last year.
- **lastTradePrice** (number) - The price of the last trade.
- **bestBid** (number) - The best bid price.
- **bestAsk** (number) - The best ask price.
- **automaticallyActive** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is automatically active.
- **clearBookOnStart** (boolean) - Indicates if the order book is cleared on start.
- **chartColor** (string) - The color used for the market's chart.
- **seriesColor** (string) - The color used for the market's series.
- **showGmpSeries** (boolean) - Indicates whether to show GMP series.
- **showGmpOutcome** (boolean) - Indicates whether to show GMP outcome.
- **manualActivation** (boolean) - Indicates if manual activation is required.
- **negRiskOther** (boolean) - Indicates negative risk for other parties.
- **gameId** (string) - The ID of the associated game.
- **groupItemRange** (string) - The range for group items.
- **sportsMarketType** (string) - The type of sports market.
- **line** (number) - The line for the market.
- **umaResolutionStatuses** (string) - UMA resolution statuses for the market.
- **pendingDeployment** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is pending deployment.
- **deploying** (boolean) - Indicates if the market is currently deploying.
- **deployingTimestamp** (string) - Timestamp when the market started deploying.
- **scheduledDeploymentTimestamp** (string) - Timestamp for scheduled market deployment.
- **rfqEnabled** (boolean) - Indicates if RFQ (Request for Quote) is enabled.
- **eventStartTime** (string) - The start time of the associated event.

#### Response Example

### GET /comments/user_address/{user_address}

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/comments/get-comments-by-user-address

Retrieves comments associated with a specific user's address. Supports filtering and pagination.

## GET /comments/user_address/{user_address}

### Description
Retrieves comments made by a specific user address. This endpoint is useful for fetching a user's comment history or activity.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/comments/user_address/{user_address}`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **user_address** (string) - Required - The wallet address of the user whose comments are to be retrieved.

#### Query Parameters
- **limit** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of comments to return. Defaults to a reasonable value.
- **offset** (integer) - Optional - The number of comments to skip before starting to collect the result set. Used for pagination.
- **order** (string) - Optional - Comma-separated list of fields to order the results by (e.g., `createdAt`).
- **ascending** (boolean) - Optional - Specifies the order direction. `true` for ascending, `false` for descending. Defaults to `false`.

### Request Example
```bash
GET https://gamma-api.polymarket.com/comments/user_address/0x123...abc?limit=10&order=createdAt&ascending=false
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
Returns an array of `Comment` objects, each containing details about a comment and its associated profile information.

- **id** (string) - The unique identifier for the comment.
- **body** (string, nullable) - The content of the comment.
- **parentEntityType** (string, nullable) - The type of entity the comment is parented to (e.g., 'market').
- **parentEntityID** (integer, nullable) - The ID of the parent entity.
- **parentCommentID** (string, nullable) - The ID of the parent comment if this is a reply.
- **userAddress** (string, nullable) - The address of the user who posted the comment.
- **replyAddress** (string, nullable) - The address of the user who this comment is replying to.
- **createdAt** (string, nullable) - The timestamp when the comment was created.
- **updatedAt** (string, nullable) - The timestamp when the comment was last updated.
- **profile** (object) - Information about the user's profile.
- **reactions** (array) - A list of reactions to the comment.
- **reportCount** (integer, nullable) - The number of times the comment has been reported.
- **reactionCount** (integer, nullable) - The total number of reactions on the comment.

#### Response Example
```json
[
  {
    "id": "cmt_12345",
    "body": "This is a great market!",
    "parentEntityType": "market",
    "parentEntityID": 67890,
    "userAddress": "0x123...abc",
    "createdAt": "2023-10-27T10:00:00Z",
    "profile": {
      "name": "PolymarketUser",
      "pseudonym": "PMUser123",
      "displayUsernamePublic": true,
      "profileImage": "https://images.polymarket.com/profile/abc.png"
    },
    "reactionCount": 5
  }
]
```

### Troubleshooting: Change Signing Server Port

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/builders/builder-signing-server

Addresses the 'listen EADDRINUSE' error by allowing users to change the port used by the Builder Signing Server. Update both the `.env` file and client configurations.

```bash
PORT=5002
```

### Configure Builder Signing Server Environment Variables

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/builders/builder-signing-server

Sets up environment variables for the Builder Signing Server, including the port and Builder API credentials. It is crucial to keep these credentials secure and not commit them to version control.

```bash
PORT=5001
POLY_BUILDER_API_KEY=your_builder_api_key
POLY_BUILDER_SECRET=your_builder_secret
POLY_BUILDER_PASSPHRASE=your_builder_passphrase
```

### GET /getPricesHistory

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/CLOB/clients/methods-public

Retrieves historical price data for a given token.

## GET /getPricesHistory

### Description
Retrieves historical price data for a token.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/getPricesHistory

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **params** (PriceHistoryFilterParams) - Required - An object containing filtering parameters for historical prices.
  - **market** (string) - Required - The token ID for which to retrieve price history.
  - **startTs** (number) - Optional - The start timestamp for the historical data (Unix timestamp in seconds).
  - **endTs** (number) - Optional - The end timestamp for the historical data (Unix timestamp in seconds).
  - **fidelity** (number) - Optional - The fidelity of the price data.
  - **interval** (PriceHistoryInterval) - Required - The time interval for the price data (e.g., 'max', '1w', '1d', '6h', '1h').

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **MarketPrice[]** - An array of market price objects, each containing `t` (timestamp) and `p` (price).

#### Response Example

```json
[
  { "t": 1678886400, "p": 1.23 },
  { "t": 1678972800, "p": 1.25 }
]
```

### Get Comments by ID - OpenAPI Specification

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/comments/get-comments-by-comment-id

This snippet defines the GET /comments/{id} endpoint in the OpenAPI 3.0.3 specification. It allows retrieval of comments associated with a specific comment ID, with an optional query parameter to include positions. The response includes detailed schema definitions for Comment, CommentProfile, Reaction, ImageOptimization, and CommentPosition objects.

```yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: Markets API
  version: 1.0.0
  description: REST API specification for public endpoints used by the Markets service.
servers:
  - url: https://gamma-api.polymarket.com
    description: Polymarket Gamma API Production Server
security: []
tags:
  - name: Health
    description: Health check endpoints
  - name: Sports
    description: Sports-related endpoints including teams and game data
  - name: Tags
    description: Tag management and related tag operations
  - name: Events
    description: Event management and event-related operations
  - name: Markets
    description: Market data and market-related operations
  - name: Comments
    description: Comment system and user interactions
  - name: Series
    description: Series management and related operations
  - name: Profiles
    description: User profile management
  - name: Search
    description: Search functionality across different entity types
paths:
  /comments/{id}:
    get:
      tags:
        - Comments
      summary: Get comments by comment id
      operationId: getCommentsById
      parameters:
        - name: id
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: integer
        - name: get_positions
          in: query
          schema:
            type: boolean
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Comments
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: array
                items:
                  $ref: '#/components/schemas/Comment'
components:
  schemas:
    Comment:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
        body:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        parentEntityType:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        parentEntityID:
          type: integer
          nullable: true
        parentCommentID:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        userAddress:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        replyAddress:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        createdAt:
          type: string
          format: date-time
          nullable: true
        updatedAt:
          type: string
          format: date-time
          nullable: true
        profile:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/CommentProfile'
        reactions:
          type: array
          items:
            $ref: '#/components/schemas/Reaction'
        reportCount:
          type: integer
          nullable: true
        reactionCount:
          type: integer
          nullable: true
    CommentProfile:
      type: object
      properties:
        name:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        pseudonym:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        displayUsernamePublic:
          type: boolean
          nullable: true
        bio:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        isMod:
          type: boolean
          nullable: true
        isCreator:
          type: boolean
          nullable: true
        proxyWallet:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        baseAddress:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        profileImage:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        profileImageOptimized:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/ImageOptimization'
        positions:
          type: array
          items:
            $ref: '#/components/schemas/CommentPosition'
    Reaction:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
        commentID:
          type: integer
          nullable: true
        reactionType:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        icon:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        userAddress:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        createdAt:
          type: string
          format: date-time
          nullable: true
        profile:
          $ref: '#/components/schemas/CommentProfile'
    ImageOptimization:
      type: object
      properties:
        id:
          type: string
        imageUrlSource:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        imageUrlOptimized:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        imageSizeKbSource:
          type: number
          nullable: true
        imageSizeKbOptimized:
          type: number
          nullable: true
        imageOptimizedComplete:
          type: boolean
          nullable: true
        imageOptimizedLastUpdated:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        relID:
          type: integer
          nullable: true
        field:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        relname:
          type: string
          nullable: true
    CommentPosition:
      type: object
      properties:
        tokenId:
          type: string
          nullable: true
        positionSize:
          type: string
          nullable: true

```

### Initialize Polymarket Relayer Client (Python)

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/builders/relayer-client

Initializes the Polymarket Relayer Client in Python. Requires environment variables for relayer URL, chain ID, private key, and builder API credentials. This client is configured for Polygon mainnet.

```python
import os
from py_builder_relayer_client.client import RelayClient
from py_builder_signing_sdk.config import BuilderConfig, BuilderApiKeyCreds

relayer_url = os.getenv("POLYMARKET_RELAYER_URL")
chain_id = 137  # Polygon mainnet
private_key = os.getenv("PRIVATE_KEY")

# Configure builder credentials
builder_config = BuilderConfig(
    local_builder_creds=BuilderApiKeyCreds(
        key=os.getenv("BUILDER_API_KEY"),
        secret=os.getenv("BUILDER_SECRET"),
        passphrase=os.getenv("BUILDER_PASS_PHRASE"),
    )
)

# Initialize client
client = RelayClient(relayer_url, chain_id, private_key, builder_config)
```

### Initialize ClobClient for Generating User API Credentials (TypeScript, Python)

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/CLOB/clients/methods-overview

Initializes the ClobClient for generating user API credentials. This requires a signer to authenticate the process. It enables access to all public and L1 methods, including functions for creating and deriving API keys.

```TypeScript
const client = new ClobClient(
  "https://clob.polymarket.com", 
  137, 
  signer
);

// All public and L1 methods available
const newCreds = createApiKey();
const derivedCreds = deriveApiKey();
const creds = createOrDeriveApiKey();
```

```Python
client = new ClobClient(
    host="https://clob.polymarket.com", 
    chain_id=137
    key="private_key"
  )

# All public and L1 methods available
new_creds = client.create_api_key()
derived_creds = client.derive_api_key()
creds = client.create_or_derive_api_key()
```

### EIP-712 Signing Example (TypeScript, Python)

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/CLOB/authentication

Demonstrates how to generate an EIP-712 signature for L1 authentication using TypeScript and Python. This involves defining a domain, types, and values for the signature structure. Ensure you have a signer object and necessary variables like chainId, signingAddress, ts, and nonce.

```typescript
const domain = {
  name: "ClobAuthDomain",
  version: "1",
  chainId: chainId, // Polygon Chain ID 137
};

const types = {
  ClobAuth: [
    { name: "address", type: "address" },
    { name: "timestamp", type: "string" },
    { name: "nonce", type: "uint256" },
    { name: "message", type: "string" },
  ],
};

const value = {
  address: signingAddress, // The Signing address
  timestamp: ts,            // The CLOB API server timestamp
  nonce: nonce,             // The nonce used
  message: "This message attests that I control the given wallet",
};

const sig = await signer._signTypedData(domain, types, value);
```

```python
domain = {
    "name": "ClobAuthDomain",
    "version": "1",
    "chainId": chainId,  # Polygon Chain ID 137
}

types = {
    "ClobAuth": [
        {"name": "address", "type": "address"},
        {"name": "timestamp", "type": "string"},
        {"name": "nonce", "type": "uint256"},
        {"name": "message", "type": "string"},
    ]
}

value = {
    "address": signingAddress,  # The signing address
    "timestamp": ts,            # The CLOB API server timestamp
    "nonce": nonce,             # The nonce used
    "message": "This message attests that I control the given wallet",
}

sig = await signer._signTypedData(domain, types, value)
```

### GET /markets

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/markets/list-markets

Retrieves a list of markets based on various filtering and sorting parameters. This endpoint is useful for fetching market data for display or analysis.

## GET /markets

### Description
Retrieves a list of markets based on various filtering and sorting parameters.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/markets

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **limit** (integer) - Optional - Maximum number of markets to return.
- **offset** (integer) - Optional - Number of markets to skip before returning results.
- **order** (string) - Optional - Comma-separated list of fields to order by.
- **ascending** (boolean) - Optional - Whether to sort in ascending order.
- **id** (array[integer]) - Optional - Filter markets by their IDs.
- **slug** (array[string]) - Optional - Filter markets by their slugs.
- **clob_token_ids** (array[string]) - Optional - Filter markets by CLOB token IDs.
- **condition_ids** (array[string]) - Optional - Filter markets by condition IDs.
- **market_maker_address** (array[string]) - Optional - Filter markets by market maker addresses.
- **liquidity_num_min** (number) - Optional - Minimum liquidity number.
- **liquidity_num_max** (number) - Optional - Maximum liquidity number.
- **volume_num_min** (number) - Optional - Minimum volume number.
- **volume_num_max** (number) - Optional - Maximum volume number.
- **start_date_min** (string) - Optional - Minimum start date (ISO 8601 format).
- **start_date_max** (string) - Optional - Maximum start date (ISO 8601 format).
- **end_date_min** (string) - Optional - Minimum end date (ISO 8601 format).
- **end_date_max** (string) - Optional - Maximum end date (ISO 8601 format).
- **tag_id** (integer) - Optional - Filter markets by tag ID.
- **related_tags** (boolean) - Optional - Whether to include related tags.
- **cyom** (boolean) - Optional - Filter by 'create your own market' status.
- **uma_resolution_status** (string) - Optional - Filter markets by UMA resolution status.
- **game_id** (string) - Optional - Filter markets by game ID.
- **sports_market_types** (array[string]) - Optional - Filter markets by sports market types.
- **rewards_min_size** (number) - Optional - Minimum rewards size.
- **question_ids** (array[string]) - Optional - Filter markets by question IDs.
- **include_tag** (boolean) - Optional - Whether to include tag information.
- **closed** (boolean) - Optional - Whether to include closed markets.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "example": "GET /markets?limit=10&order=creation_date&ascending=false"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The unique identifier for the market.
- **question** (string) - The question posed by the market (nullable).
- **conditionId** (string) - The ID of the market's condition.
- **slug** (string) - The slug for the market (nullable).
- **twitterCardImage** (string) - URL for the market's Twitter card image (nullable).
- **resolutionSource** (string) - The source for market resolution.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": [
    {
      "id": "123",
      "question": "Will Bitcoin reach $50,000 by December 31st, 2023?",
      "conditionId": "abc",
      "slug": "btc-50k-dec-2023",
      "twitterCardImage": "https://images.polymarket.com/card.png",
      "resolutionSource": "CoinGecko"
    }
  ]
}
```

### Client Initialization

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/developers/CLOB/clients/methods-l2

Initialize the ClobClient with your API credentials, signer, and funder details to authenticate requests.

## Client Initialization

L2 methods require the client to initialize with the signer, signatureType, user API credentials, and funder.

### TypeScript Example
```typescript
import { ClobClient } from "@polymarket/clob-client";
import { Wallet } from "ethers";

const signer = new Wallet(process.env.PRIVATE_KEY)

const apiCreds = {
  apiKey: process.env.API_KEY,
  secret: process.env.SECRET,
  passphrase: process.env.PASSPHRASE,
};

const client = new ClobClient(
  "https://clob.polymarket.com",
  137,
  signer,
  apiCreds,
  2, // Deployed Safe proxy wallet
  process.env.FUNDER_ADDRESS // Address of deployed Safe proxy wallet
);

// Ready to send authenticated requests to the CLOB API!
const order = await client.postOrder(signedOrder);
```

### Python Example
```python
from py_clob_client.client import ClobClient
from py_clob_client.clob_types import ApiCreds
import os

api_creds = ApiCreds(
    api_key=os.getenv("API_KEY"),
    api_secret=os.getenv("SECRET"),
    api_passphrase=os.getenv("PASSPHRASE")
)

client = ClobClient(
    host="https://clob.polymarket.com",
    chain_id=137,
    key=os.getenv("PRIVATE_KEY"),
    creds=api_creds,
    signature_type=2, # Deployed Safe proxy wallet
    funder=os.getenv("FUNDER_ADDRESS") # Address of deployed Safe proxy wallet
)

# Ready to send authenticated requests to the CLOB API!
order = await client.post_order(signed_order)
```

### Market Data Structure

Source: https://docs.polymarket.com/api-reference/series/get-series-by-id

Defines the structure for market-related data, including details about market type, event start time, and associated creators and templates.

## Market Data Structure

### Description
This structure represents the data associated with a market on the Polymarket platform. It includes various fields related to the market's configuration, event details, and associated creator and template information.

### Method
N/A (Data Structure Definition)

### Endpoint
N/A (Data Structure Definition)

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
N/A

#### Query Parameters
N/A

#### Request Body
N/A

### Request Example
N/A

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - Unique identifier for the market.
- **title** (string) - The title of the market.
- **description** (string) - A detailed description of the market.
- **slug** (string) - A URL-friendly identifier for the market.
- **image** (string) - URL of the market's image.
- **creatorId** (string) - The ID of the market's creator.
- **templateId** (string) - The ID of the market's template.
- **createdAt** (string, format: date-time) - Timestamp when the market was created.
- **updatedAt** (string, format: date-time) - Timestamp when the market was last updated.
- **outcomeType** (string) - The type of outcome for the market (e.g., 'BINARY', 'NUMERIC').
- **outcomeTitle** (string) - The title of the specific outcome.
- **volume** (number) - The trading volume of the market.
- **lastPrice** (number) - The last traded price for the market.
- **resolvedPrice** (number) - The resolved price of the market.
- **resolvedSymbol** (string) - The symbol representing the resolved outcome.
- **resolutionTime** (string, format: date-time) - Timestamp when the market was resolved.
- **status** (string) - The current status of the market (e.g., 'OPEN', 'RESOLVED').
- **category** (string) - The category the market belongs to.
- **tags** (array of strings) - Tags associated with the market.
- **initialProb** (number) - The initial probability of the market.
- **maxUsers** (number) - Maximum number of users allowed.
- **minUsers** (number) - Minimum number of users required.
- **creatorPercent** (number) - Percentage of creator fees.
- **creatorAddress** (string) - Creator's wallet address.
- **creationDate** (string, format: date-time) - Alias for createdAt.
- **marketUrl** (string) - URL to the market page.
- **marketImage** (string) - Alias for image.
- **seriesSlug** (string) - Slug for series markets.
- **seriesEndTimestamp** (string, format: date-time) - Timestamp for the end of a series.
- **seriesStartIndex** (number) - Start index for series.
- **seriesInterval** (string) - Interval for series.
- **seriesBreak** (string) - Break condition for series.
- **chartColor** (string) - Color for market charts.
- **seriesColor** (string) - Color for series charts.
- **showGmpSeries** (boolean) - Flag to show GMP series.
- **showGmpOutcome** (boolean) - Flag to show GMP outcome.
- **manualActivation** (boolean) - Flag for manual activation.
- **negRiskOther** (boolean) - Flag for negative risk on other outcomes.
- **gameId** (string) - Identifier for game-related markets.
- **groupItemRange** (string) - Range for grouping items.
- **sportsMarketType** (string) - Type of sports market.
- **line** (number) - Line value for certain market types.
- **umaResolutionStatuses** (string) - UMA resolution statuses.
- **pendingDeployment** (boolean) - Flag indicating pending deployment.
- **deploying** (boolean) - Flag indicating deployment in progress.
- **deployingTimestamp** (string, format: date-time) - Timestamp of deployment.
- **scheduledDeploymentTimestamp** (string, format: date-time) - Timestamp of scheduled deployment.
- **rfqEnabled** (boolean) - Flag indicating if RFQ is enabled.
- **eventStartTime** (string, format: date-time) - Timestamp for the start of the event.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "mk_abc123",
  "title": "Will ETH reach $5000 by EOY?",
  "description": "A market to bet on the price of Ethereum.",
  "slug": "eth-5k-eoy",

  "seriesSlug": null,
  "seriesEndTimestamp": null,
  "seriesStartIndex": null,
  "seriesInterval": null,

  "seriesColor": "#00FF00",
```

## GET /holders

GET

### Endpoint
/holders

- **market** (array[Hash64]) - Required - A comma-separated list of condition IDs.

```json
        "name": "Whale",
        "profileImage": "url/to/image.png",
        "profileImageOptimized": "url/to/optimized/image.png"
      }
    ]
  }
]
```

#### Success Response (200)
- **total** (number) - The total live volume for the event.
- **markets** (array) - An array of market volumes.
  - **market** (string) - The market identifier (Hash64).
  - **value** (number) - The volume for the specific market.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "example": [
    {
      "market": "0xdd22472e552920b8438158ea7238bfadfa4f736aa4cee91a6b86c39ead110917",
      "value": 1500.75
    }
  ]
}
```

#### Error Response (400, 500)
- **error** (string) - A description of the error that occurred.

GET

### Endpoint
/getSpreads

#### Query Parameters
